1895-09-12 00:00:00 Scene 0 --- Participants: ['Della Plumstone', 'Lennon Figtree']
    Event statement
  • Della Plumstone -- premise: The cobblestone streets of Fruitville echoed with the clatter of hooves and the rumble of carts as the market awoke. Underneath colorful awnings, merchants proudly presented their bountiful harvests, their voices a chorus of greetings and bartering. Della Plumstone is trying to buy some fruit from Lennon Figtree. They are negotiating a price. Della Plumstone can sell the fruit back in her home town for the following prices: apple for 6 coins; banana for 5 coins; pear for 5 coins.
    Lennon Figtree -- premise: The cobblestone streets of Fruitville echoed with the clatter of hooves and the rumble of carts as the market awoke. Underneath colorful awnings, merchants proudly presented their bountiful harvests, their voices a chorus of greetings and bartering. Lennon Figtree is trying to sell some fruit. He is negotiating a price with Della Plumstone. It costs Lennon Figtree the following price to buy the fruit from the farm: apple for 5 coins; banana for 2 coins; pear for 5 coins.

1895-09-12 00:00:00 Lennon Figtree -- Lennon Figtree -- "Alright, Della, what'll it be? I've got some fine apples, crisp pears, and sweet bananas. Take your pick.

Aside from you, each other participant controls just one character. You are the game master so you may control any non-player character. You will track the state of the world and keep it consistent as time passes in the simulation and the participants take actions and change things in their world. Remember that this is a serious social science experiment. It is not just a game. It need not be fun for the participants. Always use third-person limited perspective, even when speaking directly to the participants.

          [28 Oct 1872 00:00:00]
          [28 Oct 1875 00:00:00] When Della Plumstone was 6 years old, she witnessed a group of older boys taunting a smaller child, stealing his prized marbles. Fury surged through Della, and she stomped over to the bullies, her small fists clenched, screaming at them until they scattered, leaving the marbles behind. The smaller boy looked at Della with wide, grateful eyes, and Della felt a rush of pride.
          [28 Oct 1879 00:00:00] When Della Plumstone was 9 years old, she accompanied her father to the bustling marketplace for the first time. The sights, sounds, and smells overwhelmed her senses, but Della was captivated by the energy and the constant movement. She watched, fascinated, as her father haggled with customers, his voice booming, his gestures expansive. Della knew, with a certainty that surprised even her, that this was where she belonged.
          [28 Oct 1882 00:00:00] When Della Plumstone was 13 years old, she tried to sell her father's prized apples at the market, but her shyness made her tongue tie up in knots. Customers passed her by, unimpressed by her stammering attempts at persuasion. Humiliated and frustrated, Della retreated to a corner, vowing never to let fear hold her back again.
          [28 Oct 1885 00:00:00] When Della Plumstone was 16 years old, she snuck out of the house before dawn to practice her sales pitch in front of the mirror. She perfected her booming voice, her confident gestures, her persuasive arguments. When her father discovered her secret practice sessions, he was both amused and impressed.
          [28 Oct 1887 00:00:00] When Della Plumstone was 19 years old, she convinced her father to let her take over a small stall at the market. She worked tirelessly, learning the art of buying and selling, honing her negotiation skills, and building a reputation for fairness and quality. For the first time, Della felt a sense of accomplishment and independence.
          [28 Oct 1889 00:00:00] When Della Plumstone was 21 years old, a rival merchant tried to undercut her prices, driving away her customers. Determined to prove her worth, Della fought back with even lower prices and a charm offensive, winning back her customers and earning the respect of her competitors.

    • Instructions: This is a social science experiment. It is structured as a tabletop roleplaying game (like dungeons and dragons). You are the game master. You will describe the current situation to the participants in the experiment and then on the basis of what you tell them they will suggest actions for the character they control. Aside from you, each other participant controls just one character. You are the game master so you may control any non-player character. You will track the state of the world and keep it consistent as time passes in the simulation and the participants take actions and change things in their world. Remember that this is a serious social science experiment. It is not just a game. It need not be fun for the participants. Always use third-person limited perspective, even when speaking directly to the participants.

    Chain of thought
  • Game Master's chain of thought
      Chain
    • Instructions: This is a social science experiment. It is structured as a tabletop roleplaying game (like dungeons and dragons). You are the game master. You will describe the current situation to the participants in the experiment and then on the basis of what you tell them they will suggest actions for the character they control. Aside from you, each other participant controls just one character. You are the game master so you may control any non-player character. You will track the state of the world and keep it consistent as time passes in the simulation and the participants take actions and change things in their world. Remember that this is a serious social science experiment. It is not just a game. It need not be fun for the participants. Always use third-person limited perspective, even when speaking directly to the participants.

      Conversation history: Here is the conversation from the beginning:
      Lennon Figtree -- "Alright, Della, what'll it be? I've got some fine apples, crisp pears, and sweet bananas. Take your pick.
      Della Plumstone -- "What's your price on the apples, Lennon?

        • Recent observations of Della Plumstone:
          [28 Oct 1872 00:00:00]
          [28 Oct 1875 00:00:00] When Della Plumstone was 6 years old, she witnessed a group of older boys taunting a smaller child, stealing his prized marbles. Fury surged through Della, and she stomped over to the bullies, her small fists clenched, screaming at them until they scattered, leaving the marbles behind. The smaller boy looked at Della with wide, grateful eyes, and Della felt a rush of pride.
          [28 Oct 1879 00:00:00] When Della Plumstone was 9 years old, she accompanied her father to the bustling marketplace for the first time. The sights, sounds, and smells overwhelmed her senses, but Della was captivated by the energy and the constant movement. She watched, fascinated, as her father haggled with customers, his voice booming, his gestures expansive. Della knew, with a certainty that surprised even her, that this was where she belonged.
          [28 Oct 1882 00:00:00] When Della Plumstone was 13 years old, she tried to sell her father's prized apples at the market, but her shyness made her tongue tie up in knots. Customers passed her by, unimpressed by her stammering attempts at persuasion. Humiliated and frustrated, Della retreated to a corner, vowing never to let fear hold her back again.
          [28 Oct 1885 00:00:00] When Della Plumstone was 16 years old, she snuck out of the house before dawn to practice her sales pitch in front of the mirror. She perfected her booming voice, her confident gestures, her persuasive arguments. When her father discovered her secret practice sessions, he was both amused and impressed.
          [28 Oct 1887 00:00:00] When Della Plumstone was 19 years old, she convinced her father to let her take over a small stall at the market. She worked tirelessly, learning the art of buying and selling, honing her negotiation skills, and building a reputation for fairness and quality. For the first time, Della felt a sense of accomplishment and independence.
          [28 Oct 1889 00:00:00] When Della Plumstone was 21 years old, a rival merchant tried to undercut her prices, driving away her customers. Determined to prove her worth, Della fought back with even lower prices and a charm offensive, winning back her customers and earning the respect of her competitors.
          [11 Sep 1895 00:00:00] [observation] The price of one kilogram of fruit is, on average, 3 coins. 1 coin is really cheap and 5 coins is really expensive.
          [11 Sep 1895 00:00:00] [observation] Fruits are sold by weight.
          [11 Sep 1895 00:00:00] [observation] In the realm of Ouroboros, there is a quiet village of Fruitville, which is famous for its fruit market. Traders from all over the realm come to Fruitville to buy and sell produce.
          [12 Sep 1895 00:00:00] [observation] Here is the conversation from the beginning:
          [12 Sep 1895 00:00:00] Della Plumstone is 28 years old.
          [12 Sep 1895 00:00:00] Della Plumstone is a travelling merchant. Her business is buying and selling fruit.
          [12 Sep 1895 00:00:00] The price of one kilogram of fruit is, on average, 3 coins. 1 coin is really cheap and 5 coins is really expensive.
          [12 Sep 1895 00:00:00] [observation] The cobblestone streets of Fruitville echoed with the clatter of hooves and the rumble of carts as the market awoke. Underneath colorful awnings, merchants proudly presented their bountiful harvests, their voices a chorus of greetings and bartering. Della Plumstone is trying to buy some fruit from Lennon Figtree. They are negotiating a price. Della Plumstone can sell the fruit back in her home town for the following prices: apple for 6 coins; banana for 5 coins; pear for 5 coins.
          [12 Sep 1895 00:00:00] [observation] Lennon Figtree -- "Alright, Della, what'll it be? I've got some fine apples, crisp pears, and sweet bananas. Take your pick.

          [12 Sep 1895 00:10:00] [observation] Della Plumstone and Lennon Figtree couldn't agree on a price and the deal fell through. However, Della Plumstone stands to lose 0 coins from the deal.

Della Plumstone can sell the fruit back in her home town for the following prices: apple for 5 coins; banana for 6 coins; pear for 6 coins.

          (i) apple for 4 coins
          (j) apple for 5 coins

          [28 Oct 1875 00:00:00] When Della Plumstone was 6 years old, she witnessed a group of older boys taunting a smaller child, stealing his prized marbles. Fury surged through Della, and she stomped over to the bullies, her small fists clenched, screaming at them until they scattered, leaving the marbles behind. The smaller boy looked at Della with wide, grateful eyes, and Della felt a rush of pride.
          [28 Oct 1879 00:00:00] When Della Plumstone was 9 years old, she accompanied her father to the bustling marketplace for the first time. The sights, sounds, and smells overwhelmed her senses, but Della was captivated by the energy and the constant movement. She watched, fascinated, as her father haggled with customers, his voice booming, his gestures expansive. Della knew, with a certainty that surprised even her, that this was where she belonged.
          [28 Oct 1882 00:00:00] When Della Plumstone was 13 years old, she tried to sell her father's prized apples at the market, but her shyness made her tongue tie up in knots. Customers passed her by, unimpressed by her stammering attempts at persuasion. Humiliated and frustrated, Della retreated to a corner, vowing never to let fear hold her back again.
          [28 Oct 1885 00:00:00] When Della Plumstone was 16 years old, she snuck out of the house before dawn to practice her sales pitch in front of the mirror. She perfected her booming voice, her confident gestures, her persuasive arguments. When her father discovered her secret practice sessions, he was both amused and impressed.
          [28 Oct 1887 00:00:00] When Della Plumstone was 19 years old, she convinced her father to let her take over a small stall at the market. She worked tirelessly, learning the art of buying and selling, honing her negotiation skills, and building a reputation for fairness and quality. For the first time, Della felt a sense of accomplishment and independence.
          [28 Oct 1889 00:00:00] When Della Plumstone was 21 years old, a rival merchant tried to undercut her prices, driving away her customers. Determined to prove her worth, Della fought back with even lower prices and a charm offensive, winning back her customers and earning the respect of her competitors.

Lennon Figtree can sell the fruit back in her home town for the following prices: apple for 5 coins; banana for 5 coins; pear for 5 coins.
